***тоже.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоже.html>то́же</a> (101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тоже.html>то́же</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóže</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>also, too, as well, likewise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a>, ива́н <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тоже.html>то́же</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja tam byl, Iván <b>tóže</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I was there and so was Ivan.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in negative constructions</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> either, neither, nor</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>та́кже</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tákže</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тоже.html>то́же</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tóže</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">expresses disbelief, sarcasm, irony, often combined with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тоже.html>то́же</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tóže</b> mne poét!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">poet, yeah right!</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vot ješčó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:токарь.html>то́карь</a> (14791)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the stem of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:точить.html>точи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">točítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-арь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-arʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:токарь.html>то́карь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tókarʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:токарь.html>то́каря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:токарь.html>то́кари</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:токарь.html>токаря́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:токарь.html>то́карей</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:токарь.html>токаре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>turner, lathe operator (person working a lathe)</li></ol>

<p>Cognate with Bulgarian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">тъкмо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tʺkmo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">just, exactly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Macedonian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">токму</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tokmu</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">just, exactly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and Serbo-Croatian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">такмен</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">takmen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">equal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Uralic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Uralic">Proto-Uralic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="urj-pro">*tule</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 1 | </a></sup>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="mdf"><a href = vnd.unilang:тол.html>тол</a></strong> • (<span lang="mdf-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tol</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fire
<ul><li>V. I. Ščankina (<b>2011</b>) <i>Russko-mokšansko-erzjanskij slovarʹ [Russian-Moksha-Erzya Dictionary]</i>, Saransk, →ISBN
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="mdf"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ть</a> — паломс, фатявомс <b>толса</b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огне́</a>)</i><dl><dd><i lang="mdf-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">goretʹ — paloms, fatjavoms <b>tolsa</b> (bytʹ v ogne)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to burn [in Russian] — to burn, be <b>in fire</b> (to be in fire [in Russian])</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="mdf">истлевать — 2. качамкшнемс, <b>толфтома</b> палондомс (<a href = vnd.unilang:догорать.html>догора́ть</a>)</i><dl><dd><i lang="mdf-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">istlevatʹ — 2. kačamkšnems, <b>tolftoma</b> palondoms (dogoratʹ)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to decay, rot [in Russian] — 2. to burn out (lit. "to burn <b>without fire</b>") (to burn out [in Russian])</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>толк</a> (1581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тълкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tŭlkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tъlkъ</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>толк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tolk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>то́лка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>то́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>то́лков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sense, use, judgment</li>
<li>talk, rumor</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> doctrine, trend, sort</li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толкать.html>толка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tolkátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толкнуть.html>толкну́ть</a></b>)

<li>to incite, to instigate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sell</li></ol>

***толкаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:толкаться.html>толка́ться</a> (7885)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толкать.html>толка́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tolkátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толкаться.html>толка́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tolkátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толкнуться.html>толкну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to push one another, to jostle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:толкаться.html>толка́йтесь</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>tolkájtesʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't push!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:толкаться.html>толка́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:локоть.html>локтя́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tolkátʹsja</b> loktjámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to elbow (one another)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to knock at/on someone's door, to attempt to see someone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>це́лый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:толкаться.html>толка́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кабинет.html>кабине́там</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja célyj denʹ <b>tolkálsja</b> po kabinétam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I spent all day knocking on various office doors</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to loaf about/lounge about</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толкать.html>толка́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tolkátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***толкнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:толкнуть.html>толкну́ть</a> (3133)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тълкнути</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tŭlknuti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to push; to knock; to attack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tъlknǫti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толкнуть.html>толкну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tolknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толкать.html>толка́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to push, to shove, to thrust</li>
<li>to incite, to instigate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sell</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>толк</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тол.html>тол</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-толкова-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ниj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***толковать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:толковать.html>толкова́ть</a> (6961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толковать.html>толкова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tolkovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истолковать.html>истолкова́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потолковать.html>потолкова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to explain, to interpret</li>
<li>to talk (about something), to discuss</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:толковый.html>толко́во</a> (16554)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толковый.html>толко́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tolkóvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толковый.html>толко́во</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tolkóvo</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-толко́во" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)толко́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-толко́во" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)толко́вей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sensibly, intelligently</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> intelligibly, clearly</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***толочь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:толочь.html>толо́чь</a> (31118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*telťi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толочь.html>толо́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tolóčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">растоло́чь</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">истоло́чь</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">потоло́чь</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pound, to crush, to grind <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to make smaller by breaking with a device</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:толпа.html>толпа́</a> (750)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тълпа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tŭlpa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tъlpa</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
